3208    /**
3209     * Generate a sentence from this FakeLanguageGen using the specific RNG that fits in the given length limit.
3210     *
3211     * @param rng                     the RNG to use for the randomized string building
3212     * @param minWords                an int for the minimum number of words in a sentence; should be at least 1
3213     * @param maxWords                an int for the maximum number of words in a sentence; should be at least equal to minWords
3214     * @param midPunctuation          a String array where each element is a comma, semicolon, or the like that goes before a
3215     *                                space in the middle of a sentence
3216     * @param endPunctuation          a String array where each element is a period, question mark, or the like that goes at
3217     *                                the very end of a sentence
3218     * @param midPunctuationFrequency a double between 0.0 and 1.0 that determines how often Strings from
3219     *                                midPunctuation should be inserted before spaces
3220     * @param maxChars                the longest string length this can produce; should be at least {@code 6 * minWords}
3221     * @return a sentence in the gibberish language as a String
3222     */
3223    public String sentence(RNG rng, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation, String[] endPunctuation,
3224                           double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars) {
3225        if(maxChars < 0)
3226            return sentence(rng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation, midPunctuationFrequency);
3227        if (minWords < 1)
3228            minWords = 1;
3229        if (minWords > maxWords)
3230            maxWords = minWords;
3231        if (midPunctuationFrequency > 1.0) {
3232            midPunctuationFrequency = 1.0 / midPunctuationFrequency;
3233        }
3234        if (maxChars < 4)
3235            return "!";
3236        if (maxChars <= 5 * minWords) {
3237            minWords = 1;
3238            maxWords = 1;
3239        }
3240        int frustration = 0;
3241        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(maxChars);
3242        String next = word(rng, true);
3243        while (next.length() >= maxChars - 1 && frustration < 50) {
3244            next = word(rng, true);
3245            frustration++;
3246        }
3247        if (frustration >= 50) return "!";
3248        sb.append(next);
3249        for (int i = 1; i < minWords && frustration < 50 && sb.length() < maxChars - 7; i++) {
3250            if (rng.nextDouble() < midPunctuationFrequency && sb.length() < maxChars - 3) {
3251                sb.append(rng.getRandomElement(midPunctuation));
3252            }
3253            next = word(rng, false);
3254            while (sb.length() + next.length() >= maxChars - 2 && frustration < 50) {
3255                next = word(rng, false);
3256                frustration++;
3257            }
3258            if (frustration >= 50) break;
3259            sb.append(' ');
3260            sb.append(next);
3261        }
3262        for (int i = minWords; i < maxWords && sb.length() < maxChars - 7 && rng.nextInt(2 * maxWords) > i && frustration < 50; i++) {
3263            if (rng.nextDouble() < midPunctuationFrequency && sb.length() < maxChars - 3) {
3264                sb.append(rng.getRandomElement(midPunctuation));
3265            }
3266            next = word(rng, false);
3267            while (sb.length() + next.length() >= maxChars - 2 && frustration < 50) {
3268                next = word(rng, false);
3269                frustration++;
3270            }
3271            if (frustration >= 50) break;
3272            sb.append(' ');
3273            sb.append(next);
3274        }
3275
3276        if (endPunctuation != null && endPunctuation.length > 0) {
3277
3278            next = rng.getRandomElement(endPunctuation);
3279            if (sb.length() + next.length() >= maxChars)
3280                sb.append('.');
3281            else
3282                sb.append(next);
3283        }
3284
3285        if (sb.length() > maxChars)
3286            return "!";
3287        return sb.toString();
3288    }

3290    protected String[] merge1000(RNG rng, String[] me, String[] other, double otherInfluence) {
3291        if (other.length <= 0 && me.length <= 0)
3292            return new String[]{};
3293        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3294        int otherCount = (int) (1000 * otherInfluence);
3295        int idx = 0;
3296        if (other.length > 0) {
3297            String[] tmp = new String[other.length];
3298            rng.shuffle(other, tmp);
3299            for (idx = 0; idx < otherCount; idx++) {
3300                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3301            }
3302        }
3303        if (me.length > 0) {
3304            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3305            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3306            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3307                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3308            }
3309        } else {
3310            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3311                ret[idx] = other[idx % other.length];
3312            }
3313        }
3314        return ret;
3315    }

3318    protected String[] accentVowels(RNG rng, String[] me, double influence) {
3319        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3320        int otherCount = (int) (1000 * influence);
3321        int idx = 0;
3322        Matcher matcher;
3323        if (me.length > 0) {
3324            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3325            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3326            for (idx = 0; idx < otherCount; idx++) {
3327                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3328                        .replace('a', accentedVowels[0][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[0].length)])
3329                        .replace('e', accentedVowels[1][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[1].length)])
3330                        .replace('i', accentedVowels[2][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[2].length)])
3331                        .replace('o', accentedVowels[3][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[3].length)])
3332                        .replace('u', accentedVowels[4][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[4].length)]);
3333                matcher = repeats.matcher(ret[idx]);
3334                if (matcher.find()) {
3335                    ret[idx] = matcher.replaceAll(rng.getRandomElement(me));
3336                }
3337            }
3338            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3339                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3340            }
3341        } else
3342            return new String[]{};
3343        return ret;
3344    }

3391    protected String[] accentBoth(RNG rng, String[] me, double vowelInfluence, double consonantInfluence) {
3392        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3393        int idx = 0;
3394        Matcher matcher;
3395        if (me.length > 0) {
3396            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3397            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3398            for (idx = 0; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3399                boolean subVowel = rng.nextDouble() < vowelInfluence, subCon = rng.nextDouble() < consonantInfluence;
3400                if (subVowel && subCon) {
3401                    ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3402                            .replace('a', accentedVowels[0][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[0].length)])
3403                            .replace('e', accentedVowels[1][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[1].length)])
3404                            .replace('i', accentedVowels[2][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[2].length)])

3482    public FakeLanguageGen mix(FakeLanguageGen other, double otherInfluence) {
3483        otherInfluence = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(otherInfluence, 1.0));
3484        double myInfluence = 1.0 - otherInfluence;
3485
3486        RNG rng = new RNG((hash64() & 0xffffffffL) | ((other.hash64() & 0xffffffffL) << 32)
3487                ^ NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(otherInfluence));
3488
3489        String[] ov = merge1000(rng, openingVowels, other.openingVowels, otherInfluence),
3490                mv = merge1000(rng, midVowels, other.midVowels, otherInfluence),
3491                oc = merge1000(rng, openingConsonants, other.openingConsonants, otherInfluence *
3492                        Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, 1.0 - other.vowelStartFrequency + vowelStartFrequency))),
3493                mc = merge1000(rng, midConsonants, other.midConsonants, otherInfluence),
3494                cc = merge1000(rng, closingConsonants, other.closingConsonants, otherInfluence *
3495                        Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, 1.0 - other.vowelEndFrequency + vowelEndFrequency))),
3496                cs = merge1000(rng, closingSyllables, other.closingSyllables, otherInfluence *
3497                        Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, other.syllableEndFrequency - syllableEndFrequency))),
3498                splitters = merge1000(rng, vowelSplitters, other.vowelSplitters, otherInfluence);
3499
3500        IntDoubleOrderedMap freqs = new IntDoubleOrderedMap(syllableFrequencies);
3501        for (IntDoubleOrderedMap.MapEntry kv : other.syllableFrequencies.mapEntrySet()) {
3502            if (freqs.containsKey(kv.getIntKey()))
3503                freqs.put(kv.getIntKey(), kv.getDoubleValue() + freqs.get(kv.getIntKey()));
3504            else
3505                freqs.put(kv.getIntKey(), kv.getDoubleValue());
3506        }
3507        List<Modifier> mods = new ArrayList<>(modifiers.size() + other.modifiers.size());
3508        mods.addAll(modifiers);
3509        mods.addAll(other.modifiers);
3510        return new FakeLanguageGen(ov, mv, oc, mc, cc, cs, splitters, freqs,
3511                vowelStartFrequency * myInfluence + other.vowelStartFrequency * otherInfluence,
3512                vowelEndFrequency * myInfluence + other.vowelEndFrequency * otherInfluence,
3513                vowelSplitFrequency * myInfluence + other.vowelSplitFrequency * otherInfluence,
3514                syllableEndFrequency * myInfluence + other.syllableEndFrequency * otherInfluence,
3515                (sanityChecks == null) ? other.sanityChecks : sanityChecks, true, mods);
3516    }
3517
3518    private static double readDouble(Object o) {
3519        if (o instanceof Double) return (Double) o;
3520        else if (o instanceof Float) return (Float) o;
3521        else if (o instanceof Long) return ((Long) o).doubleValue();
3522        else if (o instanceof Integer) return (Integer) o;
3523        else if (o instanceof Short) return (Short) o;
3524        else if (o instanceof Byte) return (Byte) o;
3525        else if (o instanceof Character) return (Character) o;
3526        return 0.0;
3527    }
3528
3529    /**
3530     * Produces a FakeLanguageGen by mixing this FakeLanguageGen with one or more other FakeLanguageGen objects. Takes
3531     * a weight for this, another FakeLanguageGen, a weight for that FakeLanguageGen, then a possibly-empty group of
3532     * FakeLanguageGen parameters and the weights for those parameters. If other1 is null or if pairs has been given a
3533     * value of null instead of the normal (possibly empty) array of Objects, then this simply returns a copy of this
3534     * FakeLanguageGen. Otherwise, it will at least mix this language with other1 using the given weights for each.
3535     * If pairs is not empty, it has special requirements for what types it allows and in what order, but does no type
3536     * checking. Specifically, pairs requires the first Object to be a FakeLanguageGen, the next to be a number of some
3537     * kind that will be the weight for the previous FakeLanguageGen(this method can handle non-Double weights, and
3538     * converts them to Double if needed), and every two parameters after that to follow the same order and pattern
3539     * (FakeLanguageGen, then number, then FakeLanguageGen, then number...). Weights are absolute, and don't depend on
3540     * earlier weights, which is the case when chaining the {@link #mix(FakeLanguageGen, double)} method. This makes
3541     * reasoning about the ideal weights for multiple mixed languages easier; to mix 3 languages equally you can use
3542     * 3 equal weights with this, whereas with mix chaining you would need to mix the first two with 0.5 and the third
3543     * with 0.33 .
3544     * <br>
3545     * Unlike the static method {@link #mixAll(Object...)}, this _is_ intended for external use, in part because the
3546     * technique for mixing languages by weight is so much more intuitive, but also because this assigns valid data for
3547     * serializing and deserializing this FakeLanguageGen that allows it to use significantly less space (less than 1/72
3548     * the bytes used in one not-quite-simple test).
3549     *
3550     * @param myWeight the weight to assign this FakeLanguageGen in the mix
3551     * @param other1   another FakeLanguageGen to mix in; if null, this method will abort and return {@link #copy()}
3552     * @param weight1  the weight to assign other1 in the mix
3553     * @param pairs    may be empty, not null; otherwise must alternate between FakeLanguageGen and number (weight) elements
3554     * @return a FakeLanguageGen produced by mixing this with any FakeLanguageGen arguments by the given weights
3555     */
3556    public FakeLanguageGen mix(double myWeight, FakeLanguageGen other1, double weight1, Object... pairs) {
3557        if (other1 == null || pairs == null)
3558            return copy();
3559        OrderedSet<Modifier> mods = new OrderedSet<>(modifiers);
3560        FakeLanguageGen mixer = removeModifiers();
3561        FakeLanguageGen[] languages = new FakeLanguageGen[2 + (pairs.length >>> 1)];
3562        double[] weights = new double[languages.length];
3563        String[] summaries = new String[languages.length];
3564        boolean summarize = true;
3565        double total = 0.0, current, weight;
3566        languages[0] = mixer;
3567        total += weights[0] = myWeight;
3568        if ((summaries[0] = mixer.summary) == null) summarize = false;
3569        mods.addAll(other1.modifiers);
3570        languages[1] = other1.removeModifiers();
3571        total += weights[1] = weight1;
3572        if (summarize && (summaries[1] = languages[1].summary) == null) summarize = false;
3573        for (int i = 1, p = 2; i < pairs.length; i += 2, p++) {
3574            if (pairs[i] == null || pairs[i - 1] == null)
3575                continue;
3576            languages[p] = ((FakeLanguageGen) pairs[i - 1]).removeModifiers();
3577            total += weights[p] = readDouble(pairs[i]);
3578            if (summarize && (summaries[p] = languages[p].summary) == null) summarize = false;
3579        }
3580        if (total == 0)
3581            return copy();
3582        current = myWeight / total;
3583        for (int i = 1; i < languages.length; i++) {
3584            if ((weight = weights[i]) > 0)
3585                mixer = mixer.mix(languages[i], weight / total / (current += weight / total));
3586        }
3587        if (summarize) {
3588            StringBuilder brief = new StringBuilder(64);
3589            String c;
3590            int idx;
3591            for (int i = 0; i < summaries.length; i++) {
3592                c = summaries[i];
3593                idx = c.indexOf('@');
3594                if (idx >= 0) {
3595                    brief.append(c.substring(0, idx + 1)).append(weights[i]);
3596                    if (i < summaries.length - 1)
3597                        brief.append('~');
3598                }
3599            }
3600            for (int i = 0; i < mods.size(); i++) {
3601                brief.append('℗').append(mods.getAt(i).serializeToString());
3602            }
3603            return mixer.addModifiers(mods).summarize(brief.toString());
3604        } else
3605            return mixer.addModifiers(mods);
3606    }
3607
3608    /**
3609     * Produces a FakeLanguageGen from a group of FakeLanguageGen parameters and the weights for those parameters.
3610     * Requires the first Object in pairs to be a FakeLanguageGen, the next to be a number of some kind that will be the
3611     * weight for the previous FakeLanguageGen(this method can handle non-Double weights, and converts them to Double
3612     * if needed), and every two parameters after that to follow the same order and pattern (FakeLanguageGen, then
3613     * number, then FakeLanguageGen, then number...). There should be at least 4 elements in pairs, half of them
3614     * languages and half of them weights, for this to do any mixing, but it can produce a result with as little as one
3615     * FakeLanguageGen (returning a copy of the first FakeLanguageGen). Weights are absolute, and don't depend on
3616     * earlier weights, which is the case when chaining the {@link #mix(FakeLanguageGen, double)} method. This makes
3617     * reasoning about the ideal weights for multiple mixed languages easier; to mix 3 languages equally you can use
3618     * 3 equal weights with this, whereas with mix chaining you would need to mix the first two with 0.5 and the third
3619     * with 0.33 .
3620     * <br>
3621     * Not intended for external use, but it could be useful. Used internally in the deserialization code.
3622     *
3623     * @param pairs should have at least one item, and must alternate between FakeLanguageGen and number (weight) elements
3624     * @return a FakeLanguageGen produced by mixing any FakeLanguageGen arguments by the given weights
3625     */
3626    public static FakeLanguageGen mixAll(Object... pairs) {
3627        int len;
3628        if (pairs == null || (len = pairs.length) <= 0)
3629            return ENGLISH.copy();
3630        if (len < 4)
3631            return ((FakeLanguageGen) pairs[0]).copy();
3632        Object[] pairs2 = new Object[len - 4];
3633        if (len > 4)
3634            System.arraycopy(pairs, 4, pairs2, 0, len - 4);
3635        return ((FakeLanguageGen) pairs[0]).mix(readDouble(pairs[1]), (FakeLanguageGen) pairs[2], readDouble(pairs[3]), pairs2);
3636    }

3638    public FakeLanguageGen addAccents(double vowelInfluence, double consonantInfluence) {
3639        vowelInfluence = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(vowelInfluence, 1.0));
3640        consonantInfluence = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(consonantInfluence, 1.0));
3641
3642        RNG rng = new RNG((hash64() & 0xffffffffL) ^
3643                ((NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelInfluence) & 0xffffffffL) | (NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(consonantInfluence) << 32)));
3644        String[] ov = accentVowels(rng, openingVowels, vowelInfluence),
3645                mv = accentVowels(rng, midVowels, vowelInfluence),
3646                oc = accentConsonants(rng, openingConsonants, consonantInfluence),
3647                mc = accentConsonants(rng, midConsonants, consonantInfluence),
3648                cc = accentConsonants(rng, closingConsonants, consonantInfluence),
3649                cs = accentBoth(rng, closingSyllables, vowelInfluence, consonantInfluence);
3650
3651
3652        return new FakeLanguageGen(ov, mv, oc, mc, cc, cs, vowelSplitters, syllableFrequencies,
3653                vowelStartFrequency,
3654                vowelEndFrequency,
3655                vowelSplitFrequency,
3656                syllableEndFrequency, sanityChecks, clean, modifiers);
3657    }

3659    private static String[] copyStrings(String[] start) {
3660        String[] next = new String[start.length];
3661        System.arraycopy(start, 0, next, 0, start.length);
3662        return next;
3663    }

3665    public FakeLanguageGen removeAccents() {
3666
3667        String[] ov = copyStrings(openingVowels),
3668                mv = copyStrings(midVowels),
3669                oc = copyStrings(openingConsonants),
3670                mc = copyStrings(midConsonants),
3671                cc = copyStrings(closingConsonants),
3672                cs = copyStrings(closingSyllables);
3673        for (int i = 0; i < ov.length; i++) {
3674            ov[i] = removeAccents(openingVowels[i]).toString();
3675        }
3676        for (int i = 0; i < mv.length; i++) {
3677            mv[i] = removeAccents(midVowels[i]).toString();
3678        }
3679        for (int i = 0; i < oc.length; i++) {
3680            oc[i] = removeAccents(openingConsonants[i]).toString();
3681        }
3682        for (int i = 0; i < mc.length; i++) {
3683            mc[i] = removeAccents(midConsonants[i]).toString();
3684        }
3685        for (int i = 0; i < cc.length; i++) {
3686            cc[i] = removeAccents(closingConsonants[i]).toString();
3687        }
3688        for (int i = 0; i < cs.length; i++) {
3689            cs[i] = removeAccents(closingSyllables[i]).toString();
3690        }
3691
3692        return new FakeLanguageGen(ov, mv, oc, mc, cc, cs, vowelSplitters, syllableFrequencies,
3693                vowelStartFrequency,
3694                vowelEndFrequency,
3695                vowelSplitFrequency,
3696                syllableEndFrequency, sanityChecks, clean, modifiers);

3746    @Override
3747    public boolean equals(Object o) {
3748        if (this == o) return true;
3749        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
3750
3751        FakeLanguageGen that = (FakeLanguageGen) o;
3752
3753        if (clean != that.clean) return false;
3754        if (Double.compare(that.totalSyllableFrequency, totalSyllableFrequency) != 0) return false;
3755        if (Double.compare(that.vowelStartFrequency, vowelStartFrequency) != 0) return false;
3756        if (Double.compare(that.vowelEndFrequency, vowelEndFrequency) != 0) return false;
3757        if (Double.compare(that.vowelSplitFrequency, vowelSplitFrequency) != 0) return false;
3758        if (Double.compare(that.syllableEndFrequency, syllableEndFrequency) != 0) return false;
3759        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3760        if (!Arrays.equals(openingVowels, that.openingVowels)) return false;
3761        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3762        if (!Arrays.equals(midVowels, that.midVowels)) return false;
3763        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3764        if (!Arrays.equals(openingConsonants, that.openingConsonants)) return false;
3765        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3766        if (!Arrays.equals(midConsonants, that.midConsonants)) return false;
3767        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3768        if (!Arrays.equals(closingConsonants, that.closingConsonants)) return false;
3769        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3770        if (!Arrays.equals(vowelSplitters, that.vowelSplitters)) return false;
3771        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3772        if (!Arrays.equals(closingSyllables, that.closingSyllables)) return false;
3773        if (!syllableFrequencies.equals(that.syllableFrequencies)) return false;
3774        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
3775        if (!Arrays.equals(sanityChecks, that.sanityChecks)) return false;
3776        return modifiers != null ? modifiers.equals(that.modifiers) : that.modifiers == null;
3777    }

3779    @Override
3780    public int hashCode() {
3781        int result;
3782        result = CrossHash.hash(openingVowels);
3783        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(midVowels);
3784        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(openingConsonants);
3785        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(midConsonants);
3786        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(closingConsonants);
3787        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(vowelSplitters);
3788        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(closingSyllables);
3789        result = 31 * result + (clean ? 1 : 0);
3790        result = 31 * result + syllableFrequencies.hashCode();
3791        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(totalSyllableFrequency);
3792        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(vowelStartFrequency);
3793        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(vowelEndFrequency);
3794        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(vowelSplitFrequency);
3795        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(syllableEndFrequency);
3796        result = 31 * result + (sanityChecks != null ? sanityChecks.length + 1 : 0);
3797        result *= 31;
3798        if(modifiers != null) {
3799            for (int i = 0; i < modifiers.size(); i++) {
3800                result += 7 * (i + 1) * modifiers.get(i).hashCode();
3801            }
3802        }
3803        return result;
3804    }
3805    public long hash64() {
3806        long result           = CrossHash.hash64(openingVowels);
3807        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(midVowels);
3808        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(openingConsonants);
3809        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(midConsonants);
3810        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(closingConsonants);
3811        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(vowelSplitters);
3812        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(closingSyllables);
3813        result = 31L * result + (clean ? 1L : 0L);
3814        result = 31L * result + syllableFrequencies.hash64();
3815        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(totalSyllableFrequency);
3816        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelStartFrequency);
3817        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelEndFrequency);
3818        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelSplitFrequency);
3819        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(syllableEndFrequency);
3820        result = 31L * result + (sanityChecks != null ? sanityChecks.length + 1L : 0L);
3821        result *= 31L;
3822        if(modifiers != null) {
3823            for (int i = 0; i < modifiers.size(); i++) {
3824                result += 7L * (i + 1L) * CrossHash.hash64(modifiers.get(i).alterations);
3825            }
3826        }
3827        return result;
3828    }
3829
3830    @Override
3831    public String toString() {
3832        return "FakeLanguageGen{" +
3833                "openingVowels=" + Arrays.toString(openingVowels) +
3834                ", midVowels=" + Arrays.toString(midVowels) +
3835                ", openingConsonants=" + Arrays.toString(openingConsonants) +
3836                ", midConsonants=" + Arrays.toString(midConsonants) +
3837                ", closingConsonants=" + Arrays.toString(closingConsonants) +
3838                ", vowelSplitters=" + Arrays.toString(vowelSplitters) +
3839                ", closingSyllables=" + Arrays.toString(closingSyllables) +
3840                ", clean=" + clean +
3841                ", syllableFrequencies=" + syllableFrequencies +
3842                ", totalSyllableFrequency=" + totalSyllableFrequency +
3843                ", vowelStartFrequency=" + vowelStartFrequency +
3844                ", vowelEndFrequency=" + vowelEndFrequency +
3845                ", vowelSplitFrequency=" + vowelSplitFrequency +
3846                ", syllableEndFrequency=" + syllableEndFrequency +
3847                ", sanityChecks=" + Arrays.toString(sanityChecks) +
3848                ", modifiers=" + modifiers +
3849                '}';
3850    }
3851
3852    public FakeLanguageGen copy() {
3853        return new FakeLanguageGen(openingVowels, midVowels, openingConsonants, midConsonants,
3854                closingConsonants, closingSyllables, vowelSplitters, syllableFrequencies, vowelStartFrequency,
3855                vowelEndFrequency, vowelSplitFrequency, syllableEndFrequency, sanityChecks, clean, modifiers)
3856                .summarize(summary);
3857    }
3858
3859
3860    public String serializeToString() {
3861        return (summary == null) ? "" : summary;
3862    }
3863
3864    public static FakeLanguageGen deserializeFromString(String data) {
3865        if (data == null || data.equals(""))
3866            return ENGLISH.copy();
3867        int poundIndex = data.indexOf('#'), snailIndex = data.indexOf('@'), tempBreak = data.indexOf('℗'),
3868                breakIndex = (tempBreak < 0) ? data.length() : tempBreak,
3869                tildeIndex = Math.min(data.indexOf('~'), breakIndex), prevTildeIndex = -1;
3870        if (tildeIndex < 0)
3871            tildeIndex = data.length();
3872
3873        if (snailIndex < 0)
3874            return ENGLISH.copy();
3875        ArrayList<Object> pairs = new ArrayList<>(4);
3876        while (snailIndex >= 0) {
3877            if (poundIndex >= 0 && poundIndex < snailIndex) // random case
3878            {
3879                pairs.add(randomLanguage(Long.parseLong(data.substring(poundIndex + 1, snailIndex))));
3880                pairs.add(Double.valueOf(data.substring(snailIndex + 1, tildeIndex)));
3881                poundIndex = -1;
3882            } else {
3883                pairs.add(registry.getAt(Integer.parseInt(data.substring(prevTildeIndex + 1, snailIndex))));
3884                pairs.add(Double.valueOf(data.substring(snailIndex + 1, tildeIndex)));
3885            }
3886            snailIndex = data.indexOf('@', snailIndex + 1);
3887            if (snailIndex > breakIndex)
3888                break;
3889            prevTildeIndex = tildeIndex;
3890            tildeIndex = Math.min(data.indexOf('~', tildeIndex + 1), breakIndex);
3891            if (tildeIndex < 0)
3892                tildeIndex = data.length();
3893        }
3894        ArrayList<Modifier> mods = new ArrayList<>(8);
3895        if (breakIndex == tempBreak) {
3896            tildeIndex = breakIndex - 1;
3897            while ((prevTildeIndex = data.indexOf('℗', tildeIndex + 1)) >= 0) {
3898                tildeIndex = data.indexOf('℗', prevTildeIndex + 1);
3899                if (tildeIndex < 0) tildeIndex = data.length();
3900                mods.add(Modifier.deserializeFromString(data.substring(prevTildeIndex, tildeIndex)));
3901            }
3902        }
3903        FakeLanguageGen flg = mixAll(pairs.toArray());
3904        flg.modifiers.addAll(mods);
3905        return flg;
3906    }
3907
3908    public static class Modifier implements Serializable {
3909        private static final long serialVersionUID = 1734863678490422371L;
3910        public final Alteration[] alterations;
3911
3912        public Modifier() {
3913            this("[tţťțṭ]?[sśŝşšș]+h?", "th");
3914        }
3915
3916        public Modifier(String pattern, String replacement) {
3917            alterations = new Alteration[]{new Alteration(pattern, replacement)};
3918        }
3919
3920        public Modifier(String pattern, String replacement, double chance) {
3921            alterations = new Alteration[]{new Alteration(pattern, replacement, chance)};
3922        }
3923
3924        public Modifier(Alteration... alts) {
3925            alterations = (alts == null) ? new Alteration[0] : alts;
3926        }
3927
3928        public StringBuilder modify(RNG rng, StringBuilder sb) {
3929            Matcher m;
3930            Replacer.StringBuilderBuffer tb, working = Replacer.wrap(sb);
3931            String tmp;
3932            boolean found;
3933            Alteration alt;
3934            for (int a = 0; a < alterations.length; a++) {
3935                alt = alterations[a];
3936                tmp = working.toString();
3937                tb = Replacer.wrap(new StringBuilder(tmp.length()));
3938                m = alt.replacer.getPattern().matcher(tmp);
3939
3940                found = false;
3941                while (true) {
3942                    if (rng.nextDouble() < alt.chance) {
3943                        if (!Replacer.replaceStep(m, alt.replacer.getSubstitution(), tb))
3944                            break;
3945                        found = true;
3946                    } else {
3947                        if (!m.find())
3948                            break;
3949                        found = true;
3950                        m.getGroup(MatchResult.PREFIX, tb);
3951                        m.getGroup(MatchResult.MATCH, tb);
3952                        m.setTarget(m, MatchResult.SUFFIX);
3953                    }
3954                }
3955                if (found) {
3956                    m.getGroup(MatchResult.TARGET, tb);
3957                    working = tb;
3958                }
3959            }
3960            return working.toStringBuilder();
3961        }
3962

3978                new Alteration("^([aàáâãäåæāăąǻǽeèéêëēĕėęěiìíîïĩīĭįıoòóôõöøōŏőœǿuùúûüũūŭůűųαοειυаеёийъыэюяоу]+)", "$1-$1", 0.2));

3986                        + "([aàáâãäåāăąǻeèéêëēĕėęěòóôõöøōŏőǿ])"

3998         * For a language that never repeats the same letter twice in a row.
3999         */
4000        public static final Modifier NO_DOUBLES = new Modifier("(.)\\1", "$1");

4002        /**
4003         * Removes accented letters and the two non-English consonants from text generated with {@link #NORSE}.
4004         * Replaces á, é, í, ý, ó, æ, ú, and ö with a, e, i, y, o, ae, and ou. In some instances, replaces j
4005         * with y. Replaces ð and þ with th and th, except for when preceded by s (then it replaces sð or sþ
4006         * with st or st) or when the start of a word is fð or fþ, where it replaces with fr or fr.
4007         */
4008        public static final Modifier SIMPLIFY_NORSE = replacementTable(
4009                "á", "a",
4010                "é", "e",
4011                "í", "i",
4012                "ý", "y",
4013                "ó", "o",
4014                "ú", "u",
4015                "æ", "ae",
4016                "ö", "ou",
4017                "([^aeiou])jy", "$1yai",
4018                "([^aeiou])j(?:[aeiouy]+)", "$1yo",
4019                "s([ðþ])", "st",
4020                "\\bf[ðþ]", "fr",
4021                "[ðþ]", "th");
4022
4023        /**
4024         * Simple changes to merge "ae" into "æ", "oe" into "œ", and any of "aé", "áe", or "áé" into "ǽ".
4025         */
4026        public static final Modifier LIGATURES = replacementTable("ae", "æ", "oe", "œ", "[aá][eé]", "ǽ");
4027        /**
4028         * Some changes that can be applied when sanity checks (which force re-generating a new word) aren't appropriate
4029         * for fixing a word that isn't pronounceable.
4030         */
4031        public static final Modifier GENERAL_CLEANUP = replacementTable(
4032                "[æǽœìíîïĩīĭįıiùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy]([æǽœýÿŷỳy])", "$1",
4033                "q([ùúûüũūŭůűųu])$", "q$1e",
4034                "([ìíîïĩīĭįıi])[ìíîïĩīĭįıi]", "$1",
4035                "([æǽœìíîïĩīĭįıiùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy])[wŵẁẃẅ]$", "$1",
4036                "([ùúûüũūŭůűųu])([òóôõöøōŏőǿo])", "$2$1",
4037                "[àáâãäåāăąǻaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy]([æǽœ])", "$1",
4038                "([æǽœ])[àáâãäåāăąǻaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy]", "$1",
4039                "([wŵẁẃẅ])[wŵẁẃẅ]", "$1",
4040                "qq", "q");

4042        //àáâãäåāăąǻæǽaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőœǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy
4043        //bcçćĉċčdþðďđḍfgĝğġģhĥħḥjĵȷkķlĺļľŀłḷḹmṃnñńņňŋṅṇpqrŕŗřṛṝsśŝşšșṣtţťțṭvwŵẁẃẅxyýÿŷỳzźżž

4045        /**
4046         * Creates a Modifier that will replace the nth char in initial with the nth char in change. Expects initial and
4047         * change to be the same length, but will use the lesser length if they are not equal-length. Because of the
4048         * state of the text at the time modifiers are run, only lower-case letters need to be searched for.
4049         *
4050         * @param initial a String containing lower-case letters or other symbols to be swapped out of a text
4051         * @param change  a String containing characters that will replace occurrences of characters in initial
4052         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4053         */
4054        public static Modifier charReplacementTable(String initial, String change) {
4055            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[Math.min(initial.length(), change.length())];
4056            for (int i = 0; i < alts.length; i++) {
4057                //literal string syntax; avoids sensitive escaping issues and also doesn't need a character class,
4058                // which is slightly slower and has some odd escaping cases.
4059                alts[i] = new Alteration("\\Q" + initial.charAt(i), change.substring(i, i + 1));
4060            }
4061            return new Modifier(alts);
4062        }
4063
4064        /**
4065         * Creates a Modifier that will replace the nth String key in map with the nth value. Because of the
4066         * state of the text at the time modifiers are run, only lower-case letters need to be searched for.
4067         * This overload of replacementTable allows full regex pattern strings as keys and replacement syntax,
4068         * such as searching for "([aeiou])\\1+" to find repeated occurrences of the same vowel, and "$1" in
4069         * this example to replace the repeated section with only the first vowel.
4070         * The ordering of map matters if a later key contains an earlier key (the earlier one will be replaced
4071         * first, possibly making the later key not match), or if an earlier replacement causes a later one to
4072         * become valid.
4073         *
4074         * @param map containing String keys to replace and String values to use instead; replacements happen in order
4075         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4076         */
4077        public static Modifier replacementTable(OrderedMap<String, String> map) {
4078            if (map == null)
4079                return new Modifier();
4080            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[map.size()];
4081            for (int i = 0; i < alts.length; i++) {
4082                alts[i] = new Alteration(map.keyAt(i), map.getAt(i));
4083            }
4084            return new Modifier(alts);
4085        }
4086
4087        /**
4088         * Creates a Modifier that will replace the (n*2)th String in pairs with the (n*2+1)th value in pairs. Because
4089         * of the state of the text at the time modifiers are run, only lower-case letters need to be searched for.
4090         * This overload of replacementTable allows full regex syntax for search and replacement Strings,
4091         * such as searching for "([aeiou])\\1+" to find repeated occurrences of the same vowel, and "$1" in
4092         * this example to replace the repeated section with only the first vowel.
4093         * The ordering of pairs matters if a later search contains an earlier search (the earlier one will be replaced
4094         * first, possibly making the later search not match), or if an earlier replacement causes a later one to
4095         * become valid.
4096         *
4097         * @param pairs array or vararg of alternating Strings to search for and Strings to replace with; replacements happen in order
4098         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4099         */
4100        public static Modifier replacementTable(String... pairs) {
4101            int len;
4102            if (pairs == null || (len = pairs.length) <= 1)
4103                return new Modifier();
4104            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[len >> 1];
4105            for (int i = 0; i < alts.length; i++) {
4106                alts[i] = new Alteration(pairs[i<< 1], pairs[i<<1|1]);
4107            }
4108            return new Modifier(alts);
4109        }
4110
4111        /**
4112         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a vowel in addition to the vowels that the
4113         * language already uses; insertion will replace an existing vowel (at any point in a word that had a vowel
4114         * generated) with a probability of {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.1 at most) unless you want the
4115         * newly-inserted vowel to be likely to be present in every word of some sentences.
4116         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional vowel
4117         * @param chance the chance for a vowel cluster to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.1 or less
4118         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4119         */
4120        public static Modifier insertVowel(String insertion, double chance)
4121        {
4122            return new Modifier(anyVowelCluster, insertion, chance);
4123        }

4128         * a consonant generated) with a probability of {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.1 at most) unless you
4129         * want the newly-inserted consonant to be likely to be present in every word of some sentences.
4130         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional consonant
4131         * @param chance the chance for a consonant cluster to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.1 or less

4134        public static Modifier insertConsonant(String insertion, double chance)

4220                new Alteration("ā", "aa"),
4221                new Alteration("ū", "uu"),
4222                new Alteration("ī", "ii")*/);
4223
4224        @Override
4225        public boolean equals(Object o) {
4226            if (this == o) return true;
4227            if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
4228
4229            Modifier modifier = (Modifier) o;
4230
4231            // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4232            return Arrays.equals(alterations, modifier.alterations);
4233        }
4234
4235        @Override
4236        public int hashCode() {
4237            return CrossHash.hash(alterations);
4238        }
4239
4240        @Override
4241        public String toString() {
4242            return "Modifier{" +
4243                    "alterations=" + Arrays.toString(alterations) +
4244                    '}';
4245        }
4246
4247        public String serializeToString() {
4248            if (alterations == null || alterations.length == 0) return "\6";
4249            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(32).append('\6');
4250            for (int i = 0; i < alterations.length; i++)
4251                sb.append(alterations[i].serializeToString()).append('\6');
4252            return sb.toString();
4253        }
4254
4255        public static Modifier deserializeFromString(String data) {
4256            int currIdx = data.indexOf(6), altIdx = currIdx, matches = 0;
4257            while (currIdx >= 0) {
4258                if ((currIdx = data.indexOf(6, currIdx + 1)) < 0)
4259                    break;
4260                matches++;
4261            }
4262            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[matches];
4263            for (int i = 0; i < matches; i++) {
4264                alts[i] = Alteration.deserializeFromString(data.substring(altIdx + 1, altIdx = data.indexOf(6, altIdx + 1)));
4265            }
4266            return new Modifier(alts);
4267        }
4268    }
4269
4270    public static class Alteration implements Serializable {
4271        private static final long serialVersionUID = -2138854697837563188L;
4272        public Replacer replacer;
4273        public String replacement;
4274        public double chance;
4275
4276        public Alteration() {
4277            this("[tţťțṭ]?[sśŝşšș]+h?", "th");
4278        }
4279
4280        public Alteration(String pattern, String replacement) {
4281            this.replacement = replacement;
4282            replacer = Pattern.compile(pattern).replacer(replacement);
4283            chance = 1.0;
4284        }
4285
4286        public Alteration(String pattern, String replacement, double chance) {
4287            this.replacement = replacement;
4288            replacer = Pattern.compile(pattern).replacer(replacement);
4289            this.chance = chance;
4290        }
4291
4292        public Alteration(Pattern pattern, String replacement, double chance) {
4293            this.replacement = replacement;
4294            replacer = pattern.replacer(replacement);
4295            this.chance = chance;
4296        }
4297
4298        @Override
4299        public boolean equals(Object o) {
4300            if (this == o) return true;
4301            if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
4302
4303            Alteration that = (Alteration) o;
4304
4305            if (Double.compare(that.chance, chance) != 0) return false;
4306            return replacer.equals(that.replacer);
4307
4308        }
4309
4310        @Override
4311        public int hashCode() {
4312            long result;
4313            result = CrossHash.hash64(replacer.getPattern().serializeToString());
4314            result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(chance);
4315            result ^= result >>> 32;
4316            return (int) (0xFFFFFFFFL & result);
4317        }
4318
4319        @Override
4320        public String toString() {
4321            return "Alteration{" +
4322                    "replacer=" + replacer +
4323                    ", chance=" + chance +
4324                    '}';
4325        }
4326
4327        public String serializeToString() {
4328            return replacer.getPattern().serializeToString() + '\2' + replacement + '\4' + chance;
4329        }
4330
4331        public static Alteration deserializeFromString(String data) {
4332            int split2 = data.indexOf('\2'), split4 = data.indexOf('\4');
4333            return new Alteration(Pattern.deserializeFromString(data.substring(0, split2)),
4334                    data.substring(split2 + 1, split4),
4335                    Double.parseDouble(data.substring(split4 + 1)));
4336        }
4337    }
4338
4339    /**
4340     * A simple way to bundle a FakeLanguageGen with the arguments that would be passed to it when calling
4341     * {@link FakeLanguageGen#sentence(RNG, int, int, String[], String[], double, int)} or one of its overloads.
4342     * You can call {@link #sentence()} on this to produce another String sentence with the parameters it was given
4343     * at construction. The parameters to
4344     * {@link #SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen, StatefulRNG, int, int, String[], String[], double, int)} are stored in fields of
4345     * the same name, and all fields in this class are public and modifiable.
4346     */
4347    public static class SentenceForm implements Serializable
4348    {
4349        private static final long serialVersionUID = 1246527948419533147L;
4350        public StatefulRNG rng;
4351        public int minWords, maxWords, maxChars;
4352        public String[] midPunctuation, endPunctuation;
4353        public double midPunctuationFrequency;
4354        public FakeLanguageGen language;
4355
4356        /**
4357         * Builds a SentenceForm with all default fields, using {@link FakeLanguageGen#FANTASY_NAME} for a language,
4358         * using between 1 and 9 words in a sentence, and otherwise defaulting to how
4359         * {@link #SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen, int, int)} behaves.
4360         */
4361        public SentenceForm()
4362        {
4363            this(FakeLanguageGen.FANTASY_NAME, FakeLanguageGen.srng, 1, 9,
4364                    new String[]{",", ",", ",", ";", ";"},
4365                    new String[]{".", ".", ".", "!", "?", "..."}, 0.18, -1);
4366        }
4367        /**
4368         * Builds a SentenceForm with only a few fields specified. The {@link #rng} will be made based on
4369         * FakeLanguageGen's static {@link FakeLanguageGen#srng} field, maxChars will be -1 so the sentence length
4370         * will be limited only by maxWords and the length of words produced, and the between-word and end-of-sentence
4371         * punctuation will be set to reasonable defaults. This places either a comma or a semicolon after a word in the
4372         * middle of a sentence about 18% of the time ({@code midPunctuationFrequency} is 0.18), and can end a sentence
4373         * in a period, exclamation mark, question mark, or ellipsis (the "..." punctuation).
4374         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4375         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4376         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4377         */
4378        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, int minWords, int maxWords)
4379        {
4380            this(language, FakeLanguageGen.srng, minWords, maxWords, new String[]{",", ",", ",", ";", ";"},
4381                    new String[]{".", ".", ".", "!", "?", "..."}, 0.18, -1);
4382        }
4383        /**
4384         * Builds a SentenceForm with all fields specified except for {@link #rng}, which will be made based on
4385         * FakeLanguageGen's static {@link FakeLanguageGen#srng} field, and maxChars, which means the sentence length
4386         * will be limited only by maxWords and the length of words produced.
4387         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4388         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4389         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4390         * @param midPunctuation an array of Strings that can be used immediately after words in the middle of sentences, like "," or ";"
4391         * @param endPunctuation an array of Strings that can end a sentence, like ".", "?", or "..."
4392         * @param midPunctuationFrequency the probability that two words will be separated by a String from midPunctuation, between 0.0 and 1.0
4393         */
4394        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation,
4395                            String[] endPunctuation, double midPunctuationFrequency)
4396        {
4397            this(language, FakeLanguageGen.srng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation,
4398                    midPunctuationFrequency, -1);
4399        }
4400        /**
4401         * Builds a SentenceForm with all fields specified except for {@link #rng}, which will be made based on
4402         * FakeLanguageGen's static {@link FakeLanguageGen#srng} field.
4403         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4404         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4405         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4406         * @param midPunctuation an array of Strings that can be used immediately after words in the middle of sentences, like "," or ";"
4407         * @param endPunctuation an array of Strings that can end a sentence, like ".", "?", or "..."
4408         * @param midPunctuationFrequency the probability that two words will be separated by a String from midPunctuation, between 0.0 and 1.0
4409         * @param maxChars the maximum number of chars to use in a sentence, or -1 for no hard limit
4410         */
4411        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation,
4412                            String[] endPunctuation, double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars)
4413        {
4414            this(language, FakeLanguageGen.srng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation,
4415                    midPunctuationFrequency, maxChars);
4416        }
4417
4418        /**
4419         * Builds a SentenceForm with all fields specified; each value is referenced directly except for {@code rng},
4420         * which will not change or be directly referenced (a new StatefulRNG will be used with the same state value).
4421         * Note that the StatefulRandomness used by this class' rng field will always be LightRNG, even if the given rng
4422         * parameter used a different StatefulRandomness implementation.
4423         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4424         * @param rng a StatefulRNG that will not be directly referenced; the state will be copied into a new StatefulRNG
4425         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4426         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4427         * @param midPunctuation an array of Strings that can be used immediately after words in the middle of sentences, like "," or ";"
4428         * @param endPunctuation an array of Strings that can end a sentence, like ".", "?", or "..."
4429         * @param midPunctuationFrequency the probability that two words will be separated by a String from midPunctuation, between 0.0 and 1.0
4430         * @param maxChars the maximum number of chars to use in a sentence, or -1 for no hard limit
4431         */
4432        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, StatefulRNG rng, int minWords, int maxWords,
4433                            String[] midPunctuation, String[] endPunctuation,
4434                            double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars)
4435        {
4436            this.language = language;
4437            this.rng = new StatefulRNG(rng.getState());
4438            this.minWords = minWords;
4439            this.maxWords = maxWords;
4440            this.midPunctuation = midPunctuation;
4441            this.endPunctuation = endPunctuation;
4442            this.midPunctuationFrequency = midPunctuationFrequency;
4443            this.maxChars = maxChars;
4444        }
4445        public String sentence()
4446        {
4447            return language.sentence(rng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation,
4448                    midPunctuationFrequency, maxChars);
4449        }
4450
4451        public String serializeToString() {
4452            return language.serializeToString() + '℘' +
4453                    rng.getState() + '℘' +
4454                    minWords + '℘' +
4455                    maxWords + '℘' +
4456                    StringKit.join("ℙ", midPunctuation) + '℘' +
4457                    StringKit.join("ℙ", endPunctuation) + '℘' +
4458                    NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(midPunctuationFrequency) + '℘' +
4459                    maxChars;
4460        }
4461        public static SentenceForm deserializeFromString(String ser)
4462        {
4463            int gap = ser.indexOf('℘');
4464            FakeLanguageGen lang = FakeLanguageGen.deserializeFromString(ser.substring(0, gap));
4465            StatefulRNG rng = new StatefulRNG(
4466                    StringKit.longFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)));
4467            int minWords = StringKit.intFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1));
4468            int maxWords = StringKit.intFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1));
4469            String[] midPunctuation =
4470                    StringKit.split(ser.substring(gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)), "ℙ");
4471            String[] endPunctuation =
4472                    StringKit.split(ser.substring(gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)), "ℙ");
4473            double midFreq = NumberTools.longBitsToDouble(StringKit.longFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)));
4474            int maxChars = StringKit.intFromDec(ser,gap + 1, ser.length());
4475            return new SentenceForm(lang, rng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation, midFreq, maxChars);
4476        }
4477    }
4478}
